The Central Revenue Bureau has decided that all police officers in Bombay Province, in addition to ordinary police officers, will also have the power of salt tax police officers to confiscate private salt and take any other actions regarding this confiscation to counter the Gandhi movement.

Anglo-Japanese Economic Competition in India: Britain Amends Tax Rates to Exclude Japanese Goods, Causing Panic in Japan and Leading to Protests

London News: Japanese Ambassador to the UK Matsudaira was recently instructed by the Japanese government to send a note to the British Foreign Office to protest India's increase in import duties on foreign cotton fabrics. The content stated that the result of India's increase in tax rates this time is that the import tax levied on Japanese cotton fabrics is far heavier than that on British cotton fabrics, especially hindering the export of Japanese unbleached cloth to Britain. This is because the new rate stipulates that unbleached cloth is subject to an ad valorem tax of 37%, gray cloth is subject to an ad valorem tax of 27%, while British cotton fabrics are only subject to an ad valorem tax of 12% to 22%. This makes the tax levied on Japanese goods far greater than that on British goods. Last year, Japan's exports to India reached 190 million yen, of which cotton fabrics accounted for 55%, worth 108 million yen. The new Indian tariff will greatly hinder Japan's exports to Britain. A review of the amount of cotton fabrics exported to India by Britain, Japan, and China in 1929 shows that the purpose of India's tariff rate revision is to exclude Japanese cotton fabrics and replace them with British goods. Last year, from January to October, 80,552,000 yards of Japanese cotton fabrics were imported into India, 25,741,000 yards of British cotton fabrics, 15,052,000 yards of Chinese cotton fabrics, and 1,696,000 yards of cotton fabrics from other countries. Although the Japanese government does not consider the new Indian tariff rate to be a violation of the Sino-Japanese trade treaty signed in 1904, Britain sent a memorandum to Japan in 1903, asking Japan to sign the above-mentioned treaty, declaring that British and Japanese goods in the markets of both countries should be treated with absolute equality. This time, India's new tax rate aims to exclude Japanese goods and replace them with British goods, which is a great reversal of the spirit of the Anglo-Japanese trade treaty. (World News Agency)

Americans Advocate Philippine Independence; More Than 30 Groups Jointly Declare it Will Help the Success of the Naval Reduction Conference

Dentsu News Agency, New York, 14th

More than 30 agricultural and women's groups in the United States issued a joint statement saying that if they want the London Naval Conference to succeed, Philippine independence is the most urgent task. The main content is that the prerequisite for the success of the arms reduction conference is the complete independence of the Philippines. This is because the reason why the United States needs to possess a huge navy is because of the Philippines. Japan's request for 70% of the US is to seek defensive security guarantees, also because the US uses the Philippines as a base and is threatened by the US Navy. In addition, Britain's construction of a solid fortress in Singapore also targets the American forces in the Philippines. Therefore, if the Philippines is completely independent now, the arms reduction agreement between the countries can be established immediately. The people of all countries can be exempted from the heavy taxes levied for military preparations, and the agreement between the countries will feel the least difficulty. At the very least, it is hoped that the agreement between Britain, Japan, and the United States can be established.

Unemployment Continues to Increase in Japan; 310,000 Investigated at the End of Last Year; The Actual National Number is About 700,000 to 800,000

World News Agency: According to a survey by the Social Affairs Bureau of the Japanese Ministry of Internal Affairs on the unemployment situation in six major cities and the whole country, on December 1 last year, among the 6,941,937 people surveyed, there were 315,269 unemployed people, and the unemployment rate was 4.54%, an increase of 15,074 people from the previous month, or 0.28%. From the perspective of the type of unemployment, the unemployment rate of day laborers is still the highest (unemployment number 120,759, unemployment rate 7.67). Among the main prefectures, Tokyo (78,490) and Osaka (28,990) have the most. The actual number of unemployed people nationwide is about 700,000 to 800,000. Based on this survey, the bureau plans to cooperate with relevant government agencies and social and business groups to carry out unemployment prevention projects.

Yesterday, in the manager's stock store area of Kabutocho, Nihonbashi, someone distributed leaflets plotting to disrupt the financial world, causing a great commotion. Educational News

The Fourth Day of the Citywide Games

▲Men's Basketball Championship – East-West

▲Women's Volleyball Championship – Minli

▲Today's Men's Volleyball Final

The Shanghai Citywide Games were held for the fourth day yesterday, featuring six events including swimming, baseball, men's and women's basketball, soccer, women's volleyball, and tennis. The number of spectators at each venue was even greater than before, numbering approximately 20,000. In the end, Jiaotong University team won the baseball championship, East-West won the men's basketball championship, Minli won the women's volleyball championship, and Lu Yishen won first place in swimming. The details are recorded below.

Men's Basketball: Intense Battle Between Qingguang and East-West

East-West Wins the Championship

▲Forty-Two to Forty-One

▲The Difference Between the Two Sides Was Only One Point

In the basketball final between East-West and Qingguang, with only fifteen seconds remaining, East-West was ahead by one point, with a score of forty-two to forty-one. At that moment, East-West's Huang Yunli was penalized for a foul, and Qingguang's Li Baojun was about to take the free throw. As he prepared to shoot, the thousands of spectators in the stands shouted with all their might, shaking the roof tiles. The sense of urgency was difficult to describe. Qingguang and Li himself were filled with intense hope for victory. As he raised his hand to shoot, he couldn't help but tremble. The ball was released, but it missed. Qingguang was defeated by one point, which could be considered unfortunate. If that ball had gone in, Qingguang's momentum would have surged, turning defeat into victory, or even possibly winning.

▲Both Sides Had Their Own Distinctive Tactics

Both sides played with great skill. Qingguang's game was full of fighting spirit and courage. Their advances and retreats were full of passion and energy. Their actions were quite formidable. East-West's tactics were characterized by meticulous play and balanced strength. Each had its own advantages and distinctive features. In terms of defense, Qingguang's Kong Guangyi and Li Baojun were truly formidable. Their contributions to the game were significant. However, apart from Tan Dahua, the other two forwards, Huang Xishu and Chen Hualu, seemed too weak. This was where they lost. On the East-West side, Chen Zhongen was the most outstanding, without any flaws. Qu Hongren's defense was also commendable. The forwards Huang Yunli and Liang Guoquan both performed well, but He Tong showed some fatigue.

▲Coming from Behind, They Maintained the Advantage

Tan Dahua, Chen Hualu, and Kong Guangyi successively scored three baskets, giving Qingguang a great start with a six-to-zero lead. Under this pressure, East-West fought hard, and Chen Zhongen, Huang Lianli, and He Tong successively broke through, turning the score around to nine to six, taking the lead. From then on, they maintained the advantage. However, the score difference was minimal. They persevered for a long time, reaching seventeen to sixteen, with East-West leading by only one point. Continuing their efforts, Huang Yunli made a free throw, and Liang Guoquan and He Tong also scored, giving them a twenty-two to sixteen lead at halftime.

▲The One-Point Difference Could Not Be Recovered

After the break, Qingguang immediately caught up. Tan, Chen, and Kong all made contributions. The shouts of "Qingguang! Qingguang!" echoed from the stands. The atmosphere became heated, and the situation became urgent. After a while, the East-West team continued to advance and rise. Qingguang repeatedly requested timeouts to slow down the momentum. Indeed, their spirits were revived, and they tied the score at thirty-five. For a moment, the cheers and shouts were deafening. Such was their enthusiasm. Soon after, East-West took the lead again, scoring forty-two points. The youth team used all their strength to catch up, scoring forty-one points. East-West's Huang Yunli committed a foul, but Li Baojun missed the free throw, causing them to lose by one point and finish as runners-up. The referee was Zhang Guoxun.

Women's Volleyball: Minli Wins the Championship

▲Yesterday, They Defeated Wuben Two to Zero

At half past one yesterday afternoon, referee Jiang Xiangqing gave the order from the high platform, and Pei Xiyuan recorded the scores from the side. Wuben team won the right to choose sides and decided to line up on the south side of the field. Once the positions were arranged, the whistle blew, and the battle began.

▲After Several Fierce Battles, Minli Wins the First Set

Minli's Yin Linzhen served the first ball. Wuben's players crouched and waited to receive, still quite poised. After a few exchanges, Wuben took an early lead of three points, which boosted their morale. However, they still faced counterattacks, hoping to regain the lead. Although Minli had many seasoned players, they could not easily achieve their goals. Both sides exchanged serves, continuing the game. Sometimes they scored two points, sometimes one, and sometimes none. It wasn't that their serving skills were not refined, but that the attacks were all strong. When Minli reached eleven points, they switched sides. The server had already been through eight people. At that time, Wuben also got six points. With the whistle blowing in continuous battles, Wuben improved greatly. Li Bo's backhand pass, Zhang Biru's jumping block, Xue Zhijie's two-handed smash, and Shen Zuxia and Wang Xuehua's timely support all showed their expertise. Minli's Su Zuqi and Wang Dale's multiple spikes, and Yu Xuhuai and Tao Chun's receptions also showed their prowess. The ball moved back and forth, rising and falling, changing magically. The players jumped and dived, busy all the time. The spectators sitting on the stands also responded with bursts of applause. After a chaotic battle, Wuben's score increased, making the score thirteen to ten. The difference was only three points.

Unfortunately, luck was not on their side. Minli's Yu Qihuai, following Tao Chun, served from the side with great ferocity. Zhu Minbao, Zhu Youlan, Chen Caifeng, and others also helped in the battle, adding six consecutive points, reaching twenty-one. At that time, Wuben had eleven points. Minli won the first game and took the lead.

Going with the Flow, Wuben Lost Again

After a short rest, they lined up again to fight. Wuben's Li Bo served, accurately and powerfully. Unfortunately, after scoring two points, it was interrupted. Minli's Su Zushi stepped up to replace her, but did not achieve success. In a flash, the right to serve fell into the hands of Minli's Wang Dale, who scored ten consecutive points. After Zhu Shangfu changed hands, Minli's captain, Su Zuqi, came out to serve, turning over and shooting like a swift falcon, gaining one point and taking the upper hand. The momentum became even stronger. Although Wuben had many strong players, it was difficult to resist. With a quick advance of eleven points, they won another game. At that time, Wuben only got three points.

▲Baseball Championship – Jiaotong University

▲Swimming First Place – Yu Binqi

▲Men's and Women's Tennis Singles Finals

▲Baseball Game

▲Jiaotong University Defeats Fudan to Win the Championship

▲Thirteen to Four

The Jiaotong University baseball team enjoys a good reputation in Shanghai, mainly because it has a wealth of talent and has been well-trained. Jiaotong University's pitcher was Lu Jicang, and the catcher was Fei Fuxu. They cooperated well. Fudan's pitcher was Ren Zhongling, and the catcher was Zhou Chongdao. They were not weak either. Yesterday's Women's Basketball Game

Southeast Wins Second Place

Sixteen to Fifteen Victory Over Liangjiang

In the women's basketball championship competition, Southeast lost to Six Stars, and although Liangjiang beat Six Stars, it was penalized by the organizing committee due to the eligibility of its players, and was therefore disqualified, allowing Six Stars to win the championship. Last night, Southeast and Liangjiang competed for second place at the China Basketball Hall. In the end, Southeast won by one point, with a score of sixteen to fifteen.

Although Liangjiang's Zhan Jun was disqualified, Yang Pingang's skills were excellent, surpassing Zhan Jun. Both the forwards and guards were well-connected, and they had sufficient strength. Therefore, after the start of the game, Liangjiang took the lead all the way, with great momentum. At the most, the score difference was six or seven points. Unexpectedly, in the last quarter, Southeast's momentum suddenly surged, and the score increased continuously. Finally, Dun Xiaoping scored a long shot, resulting in a comeback victory for Southeast by one point, which can be described as fortunate.

Both teams had good connections and strong defenses. Liangjiang's forwards were very brave, and Shao Jinying was particularly outstanding. Southeast's defense was negligent, so in the first half, Liangjiang took the lead with nine to four. In the second half, Southeast's Qian Qizhen was transferred to the defense, and the strength suddenly increased.

Wu and Jiang became more and more skilled, making it difficult for Liangjiang's forwards to penetrate their defenses. The forwards focused on offense. The center Guo Xiaoping was lively and resilient, scoring ten points alone, turning the tide. Her contribution was the greatest. Not long after the start of the game, Southeast's Guo scored the first point, but from then on, Liangjiang took the lead all the way, and Southeast was difficult to follow. In the first quarter, the score was three to two. In the second quarter, it was six to two. In the first half, Liangjiang scored a total of nine points, while Southeast only scored four. In the second half, after Southeast's ball changed the defense and became solidified, and the forward Guo made many miraculous contributions, the score gradually approached. The atmosphere of the court also became tense. At the end of the first half, Southeast was only two points behind, with Liangjiang leading twelve to ten.

After the break, the two sides battled for a long time, tying the score at twelve to twelve. Southeast was pleased. Liangjiang's Shao Xiying scored another goal, so Liangjiang still led by two points. However, Southeast was not discouraged and worked hard to counterattack. Yang Mingqing added two points, making the score fourteen to fourteen. Soon after, Southeast's Guo Xiaoping made a long shot, hitting the target. Therefore, Southeast was two points ahead. At that time, the competition was fierce, and the shouts of the audience made the atmosphere more urgent. Although Liangjiang made a free throw, time was up, and there was no chance to overtake. In the end, Southeast won sixteen to fifteen. The referee was Song Junfu.

Soccer Preliminary Round: Huale Wins Over Youyou

Result: Five to Three

Effortlessly Securing a Spot in the Finals Due to Jiaotong University's Withdrawal

In the warm spring breeze and bright sunshine yesterday afternoon, the Huale soccer team defeated the Youyou team by a score of five to two. Because Jiaotong University withdrew from the game against Jinan today, Huale secured a spot in the finals. Several thousand spectators watched, which can be said to be a grand occasion. The referee was Le Xiurong.

Huale Receives Unexpected Support from the Audience

Among the audience, there seemed to be a misunderstanding, thinking that Huale was the same as the Lehua soccer team.

In fact, this is not the case. The Huale team is a mixed team composed of several Lehua team members and several Shanghai University team members. The audience loved Lehua so much that they cheered wildly when Huale won and sighed when Huale lost. They were happy when Huale prospered and worried when Huale was in danger. Huale was able to win because of this unexpected support from over a thousand people.

Youyou Dominated the First Half

Generally speaking, Youyou was stronger than Huale in the first half. The ball was mostly in Huale's territory. Unfortunately, Youyou's forwards seemed to lack agility. Moreover, Huale's goalkeeper, Zhou Xianyan, was like a one-man army, and Sun Sijing, the center back, handled the situation well, which was a major obstacle for Youyou.

Huale Was Stronger Than Youyou in the Second Half, Launching a Large-Scale Offensive. Youyou's Goalkeeper Was Far Inferior to Zhou Xianyan.

At the start of the game, the two sides attacked each other. Youyou launched the first offensive, attacking fiercely in one go. However, Huale's defense was tight, and there was no gap to take advantage of. Huale's offense was inferior to its defense, so only Youyou's forwards were able to roam freely in Huale's territory. After twenty minutes, Youyou's right winger, Shao Leping, flew in from the right, and Yu Guanghui kicked the ball, scoring one goal. Huale countered, and Qian Jingfu also scored a goal, making the score one to one. Youyou's left winger, Lu Wenxiang, scored another goal, making the score two to one in the first half, with Youyou winning.

Five to Three: Huale Wins Over Youyou Team

After a short break, Huale got a chance to advance, and left winger Lu Wenxiang made a contribution, making the score two to two. After a long time of stalemate, Huale's center back Sun Sijing kicked the ball from a long distance, flying from thirty yards away. Youyou's goalkeeper thought the ball would go out, but it accidentally brushed the wooden net. Huale won three to two. Youyou attacked to Huale's goal, and the inner guard committed a foul. Youyou's center forward, Xi Qiaosheng, kicked a twelve-yard ball, scoring in one go, making the score three to three. After that, Huale's momentum turned strong, and Huang Jiaoyan, Liu Xinghua, and Wu Jian made miraculous contributions. Huale won five to three.

Yesterday's Tennis Match

(1) Men's Singles:

Yu Tianguang Defeats Shen Meizhen: 6-4, 6-0

Li Huitang Defeats Zheng Guangyuan: 3-6, 6-1, 6-4

Zheng Zhaojia Defeats Qian Yaobin: 6-4, 6-3

Wu Shaoxiang Defeats Yan Rongsheng: 6-2, 6-3

The four quarterfinal matches yesterday were evenly matched. For example, Yan Rongsheng, who had won the Shanghai championship for three consecutive years, unexpectedly lost to Wu Shaoxiang by a score of 2-6, 3-6, which was unexpected by most people. Wu is a veteran in the tennis world. In 1920, he teamed up with Diao Qinghuan to defeat Shi Changli and Zhang Zizhen to win the Shanghai doubles championship. Later, Wu went to Java, so few people in Shanghai knew Wu Shaoxiang. Wu's stroke skills are very good. As for Yan Rongsheng's defeat, it was due to the lack of training due to the seasonal relationship. Yu Tianguang's victory over Shen Meizhen also showed good performance. Yu is young and handsome and is the flower of tennis, and his future is limitless.

(2) Women's Singles:

Li Lian Defeats Kuai Shuping: 3-6, 8-6, 6-1

Qiu Fumin Defeats Chen Xinyuan: 6-0 (Retired)

Among the two women's singles matches, the group of Li Lian and Kuai Shuping was remarkable. Ms. Li had just returned from abroad and had superb skills. Everyone wanted to see her first performance. Ms. Kuai Shuping, who was a dark horse, was well-trained in tennis, and her hitting skills were sophisticated, accurate, urgent, and powerful. Her serve and stroke skills were all excellent. Yesterday, she almost defeated Li Lian. Ms. Li Lian's tennis skills, all kinds of hitting skills, seemed to be inferior to Kuai, but her will to be calm and composed was her specialty. As for Kuai's failure, it was due to her weakness and the fact that she had practiced with another man and woman for an hour before the start of the game, which made her tired during the official game, which was a pity.

No Soccer Game Today: Jiaotong University Cannot Attend, Jinan Gets the Right to the Finals

The soccer game was divided into two preliminary groups. One group was held yesterday, and Huale won against Youyou. The other group was originally scheduled to be held today, but Jiaotong University was unable to attend due to academic reasons. Several players were unable to play, and they informed the organizing committee in advance. Therefore, Jinan got the right to the finals and will compete with Huale for the championship at 4:00 PM tomorrow afternoon.

Suzhong Men's and Song Women's Middle School Are Currently Ranked First: Awards to be Given Today

At the same time, in the afternoon, the ball games of the public preliminary meeting will also begin to proceed. The enthusiasm of the participants and the number of events are even more than yesterday.

Resolutions of the General Meeting

Those Who Have Participated in the Shanghai City Competition Do Not Need to Come to Zhen: Xia Kaiming's 100-Meter Final Rights are Canceled, Discussion on the Distribution of Awards

Awards Meeting: Chu Minyi presided over this conference’s awards meeting. The applicants from various departments were very enthusiastic, which was the most unique aspect of this conference.

A meeting was convened last night to discuss the distribution of awards. The General Assembly decided that those who participated in the Beijing-Shanghai special city preliminary meeting and did not come would be telegraphed to stop coming to Zhen. Those who have already come are temporarily allowed to compete and will be handled by the selection committee at its discretion. The Shanghai Qingguang team will have difficulty coming to Zhen to attend.

The order of the seventh day is as previously mentioned.

The General Assembly received a telegram from Chu Minyi stating that he has recovered from his illness and will be allowed to come to Zhen on the 17th. Xia Kaiming's 100-meter final rights were canceled after several judicial meetings decided.

Three New Records Were Created in the Last Two Days: 100 Meters, Shot Put, Triple Jump

A total of sixteen finals were held on the 15th and 16th. Among the six men's items, three new records were created: 100 meters in 12.1 seconds, shot put at 11.103 meters, and triple jump at 11.23 meters. High jump was the same as the previous edition, and pole vault seemed to be weakened. The Group B 400 meters, shot put, and discus were also new records. The high jump and long jump were not as good as before. In general, yesterday's performance was quite satisfactory, and there may be even better results today.

Wonderful Performance

National Art Performance: On the afternoon of the second day, the Jiangsu Provincial National Art Museum performed. The entire National Art team had more than one hundred people. The most exciting performances were Tai Chi Sword, Xingyi Quan, and Chain Fist.

Women's School Performance: Wuxi Jingzhi Women's School performed group exercises in the afternoon with white hats and blue dresses. The whole audience was touched, and the performance became more brilliant. The audience praised it. Danyang Zhengze Women's School performed freehand exercises in the afternoon, with graceful figures and excellent postures, which were rare performances. The instructor was Jiang Yunhe.

The guests applauded and cheered, creating a lively and bustling atmosphere, truly reaching a peak for a moment. After the ceremony, everyone gathered for a group photo. The guests enjoyed champagne and refreshments, and Mr. Lu Bohong, representing the company, delivered the following speech in Chinese and French: "Today is the launching ceremony of our Yong'an Steamer. We are honored and deeply grateful that you have all graced us with your presence. Considering that the current ships sailing the Haizhou route are old-fashioned and slow, making it difficult to compete with foreign ships, our company gathered like-minded individuals last year to establish the Da Zhen Shipping Company. We commissioned the Qiu Xin Shipyard to build two shallow-draft, steel-hulled, fast steamers, equipped with two of the most famous German Meng'An Company's new diesel engines, each with 820 horsepower, capable of traveling at 10 nautical miles per hour. These ships will operate on the Shanghai-Haizhou route, facilitating transportation and promoting the development of Haizhou's commercial shipping. The ships are equipped with wireless communication, have a draft of 11 feet, and a carrying capacity of 1,500 tons. They feature spacious dining rooms, official cabins, and other amenities to accommodate passengers. They are not only suitable for the Shanghai route but also for the Northern and Southern Seas, such as Qingdao, Tianjin, and various Yangtze River ports. The future development of transportation can be confidently anticipated. The Qiu Xin Shipyard's construction of our two ships showcases modern techniques and robust engineering. We hope that other shipping companies will also commission vessels from this shipyard. In the coming years, our company plans to order more ships from this shipyard to revitalize China's shipping industry. Our company is in its initial stages, with much to be done. We humbly request that guests provide guidance and support. With this toast, I wish Qiu Xin Shipyard prosperous business, Da Zhen Shipping Company flourishing shipping operations, and all guests boundless happiness and robust health."

The Distant Memorial Service of Master Shandao

Yesterday, Buddhists held a service at Jingye Temple to commemorate Tang Dynasty Master Shandao, the second patriarch of the Chinese Pure Land School. Master Shandao's contribution to the eastward transmission of Buddhism was immense. He left behind scriptures such as "Exhortations to the World" and "Mirror of Mindfulness of the Buddha," which have spread throughout East Asia. Believers in Japan regard him as the first patriarch of the Pure Land School. March 16th marks the 1,250th anniversary of the master's passing. Fellow Buddhists in Shanghai held a distant memorial service at the Buddhist Jingye Temple on Hart Road, piously performing rituals. Many Japanese male and female believers, deeply grateful for Master Shandao's great kindness in spreading the Dharma eastward, also participated in the worship.

Scare-Fraud Gang Repeatedly Commits Crimes: Sentenced to One Year and Six Months in Prison

Xue Gensheng, a cold-work foreman at the Rui Rong Iron Factory, was intimidated and defrauded by Dai Achang from Wuxi and his gang on the night of the 3rd of this month. The Huishan Police Department arrested Dai and brought him to the Provisional Court for investigation. The police have now determined that the suspect had previously organized gangs for robbery, extortion, and intimidation on at least four occasions. The witnesses were summoned the other day, and the defendant was brought to court. Judge Xu presided over the continuing trial. The witness, Fan Chen, testified that she lived in the same house as the plaintiff and personally heard the defendant demanding money from Xue's wife, threatening to resort to drastic measures if she did not comply. Xue had not yet returned home at that time. He A'da also testified that he had witnessed the defendant demanding money from Xue on Wuzhou Road. The defendant continued to be evasive. After arguments between the plaintiff's lawyer, Fan Gang, and the defendant's lawyer, Judge Xu sentenced Dai Achang to one year and six months in prison as a warning.

The Actor Liu Fuchu, Who Abused His Apprentice to Death, is Arrested

Tao Zhao's 14-year-old son, Tao Juming, was apprenticed to the actor Li Ruiting. Later, Li went to Suzhou and entrusted his brother-in-law, Liu Fuchu (also known as Liu Yuying), to teach him. Unexpectedly, Juming was injured and died. Tao Zhao sued Li and Liu in the Provisional Court. Liu evaded arrest, while Li and his wife, Liu Lianxiang, were interrogated and released. Warrants were issued for the arrest of Liu and Tao Wanxing for further investigation. As reported in previous newspapers, on the 13th of this month, Liu Fuchu appeared in the rooftop garden of the Sincere Department Store and was recognized by Bao Tan Che Xueceng of the Xinzha Police Department, who immediately arrested him. He was brought to court the other day, interrogated by Judge Sun, and ordered to be detained pending a scheduled trial by Judge Tan, who originally heard the case.

Western Woman Injured by Car: Driver Released on Bail Pending Trial

Gao En, a Westerner, hired a lawyer to file a complaint in the French Concession court, stating that the plaintiff's wife, Fiya Gaolun, was walking on Baochang Road at around 7:00 PM on the 12th of this month when she was struck by a car driven recklessly by the driver Xu A'er, causing her to fall and be injured. She was taken to the hospital for treatment but has not fully recovered. He requested an investigation. The defendant, Xu A'er, stated that the car belonged to Director Chen of the Third Section of the Shanghai Special City Public Security Bureau. On that day, a civilian drove the car and caused the accident. Chinese and Western officials ordered Xu to pay 200 yuan in silver and post bail, pending an inquiry to the Public Security Bureau regarding the car's insurance policy and the owner of the car. Further investigation will then be conducted.

Car Kills Pedicab Driver: Car Owner Ordered to Pay 300 Yuan in Compensation

Jin Genxiang, the assistant driver of car owner Wu Laifu, a wealthy man residing at 759 Mette He Si Tuo Road in the Public Concession, drove the car without permission on the morning of the 11th of last month to Mai Er Xi Ai Road in the French Concession. Due to inexperience, he struck and killed Jia Fayou, who was pushing a pedicab, and injured another person. The police arrested Jin and sent him to the French Concession court, which sentenced him to imprisonment. Subsequently, the families of the deceased and the injured jointly hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit seeking compensation. Wu also hired a lawyer to defend him. The court ordered a hearing. The other day, the Chinese and Western officials of the Chamber of Commerce summoned both parties and ruled that the car owner, Wu Laifu, was undeniably at fault and should compensate the family of the deceased with 300 yuan and the injured party with 50 yuan.

University Student Injures Person While Riding Motorcycle

Tang Meizhou, a student at Chi Zhi University in Jiangwan, originally from Guangdong, was riding his self-owned No. 101 motorcycle at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Bazhi Road yesterday at around 3:15 PM when he struck Zhou Acha, a 59-year-old man from Songjiang, due to excessive speed. Zhou suffered a head injury and bled profusely. Officer No. 521 arrested Tang and sent the injured man to Tongren Hospital for treatment.

Strange Incident of Dog Feces Stuffed in Mouth: Zhu Mu Also Tastes Strange Flavor; Is it Related to Lawsuit?

Zhu Mu, originally from Hubei, was involved in a lawsuit regarding withdrawal of shares in the Civil Court of the District Court the other day. After the hearing ended at 3:00 PM, he was waiting for a tram at the train station, intently watching for its arrival. Unexpectedly, a man suddenly approached and stuffed a package of dog feces wrapped in oil paper into Zhu's mouth, causing Zhu to taste the unpleasant flavor. Zhu managed to apprehend the man and filed a complaint with the District Court. The man, named Wang Jianqing, vehemently denied the act. The prosecutor interrogated Wang and ordered him to be detained, charging him with public insult.

Zhao Hanren Loses Wife, Regains Wife: Jin A'jin Flees

Zhao Hanren, who owns the Zhao Rongcheng tofu shop in Lujia Village, Pudong, has a 17-year-old wife, Shen, who was recently married. She was enticed into adultery by Jin A'jin, who lived nearby, and was brought to Shanghai and hidden at the home of Jin A'jin's maternal uncle, Wu Laisheng, in Xiejiaqiao Lujiabang. The other day, Zhao found out and indeed saw his wife inside, but A'jin had already fled. Zhao then arrested Wu and his wife and brought them to the Second District Police Station, which transferred them to the District Court for investigation.

Shi Jinqi Suddenly Abducted: Neighbor Tao Genfu is Suspicious

Shi Heshang, a local resident living near Guangyi Hospital on Robert Road in the western part of Shanghai, has a six-year-old son, Jin Hai, who is clever and lively. Shi cherishes him. Unexpectedly, he was suddenly abducted on the 11th of this month. Shi found that Shen Rong's second son, Shen Genfu, a neighbor, had also disappeared. He suspected that Genfu was involved. He questioned Shen Rong and his eldest son, A'gen. A'gen promised to find him, but A'gen also disappeared. Shi Heshang knew that his suspicions were correct and arrested Shen Rong and brought him to the Sixth District. He was sent to the District Court for interrogation yesterday.

Taoist Priest's Divorce Issue: Jin Junde Wants to Divorce Wife; Zhu Qiuyun Still Insists on Cohabitation

Jin Junde, a Taoist priest from Xiaojing Genglang, located east of Beixinjing in the northwestern countryside of this county, recently hired a lawyer to file a divorce lawsuit in the District Court. His reasons were that his wife, Zhu Qiuyun, insulted her elders, was unchaste, shrewish, unreasonable, destroyed property, neglected household duties, and frequently resorted to violence. The defendant, Zhu Qiuyun, also hired lawyer Wang Chengkuan to file a counterclaim requesting cohabitation. Judge Zhao opened the court yesterday to hear the case. The plaintiff, Jin Junde, did not appear. Only the defendant, Zhu Qiuyun, and lawyer Wang came to court. The defendant was short in stature and plainly dressed. She appeared to be a timid villager, not a shrew. She testified that she was 30 years old, a local, and lived in Xiaojing Genglang, east of Beixinjing. (Question) When did you get married? (Answer) I got married on the third day of the eleventh month when I was 17 years old. (Question) Your husband wants to divorce you. What do you think? (Answer) I don't want to. (Question) Do you have any children? (Answer) I have had five pregnancies, two of which were unsuccessful. I currently have three children: a daughter who is 10 years old, a son who is 7 years old, and the youngest son is 4 years old. (Question) Does your husband treat you well? (Answer) He was good to me at first, but since he had an affair the year before last, he often beats me. His mistress is named Xiufang, and her surname is Nie, I don't know. (Question) What does your husband do for a living? (Answer) He is a Taoist priest. (Question) Do you have parents-in-law? (Answer) I only have a mother-in-law. (Question) Do you get along well with your mother-in-law? (Answer) Yes, my mother-in-law treats me very well. (Question) Who does the housework? (Answer) My mother-in-law and I do it together. (Question) Have you ever hit your husband? (Answer) Sir, you can see that I am short and a good person. I am already happy that he doesn't hit me. How could I hit him? When he hits me, I just step aside and never hit back. (Question) Do you live with your husband now, or do you live separately? (Answer) I live with my mother-in-law in Xiaojing Genglang, and he lives with his mistress in Beixinjing. At this point, lawyer Wang said, "In April of the 17th year of the Republic of China, the plaintiff took the defendant to the Baohe Hotel in Shanghai and asked someone to sell the defendant to Baoshan. Later, the defendant escaped back home. The plaintiff's behavior is outrageous. Moreover, the defendant already has three children. The plaintiff's request for divorce is completely unreasonable. I request that it be rejected." The judge said that it was necessary to summon the plaintiff's mother to court to prove whether there was any insult or abuse and ordered the defendant to leave and await a hearing and decision.

Until Auspicious Times Arrive, A Woman Departs Afar: Hou Jinsheng Cannot Marry Wife; Wang A'san Flees Without a Trace

Hou Jinsheng, from Shengliu Township in southern Shanghai, works as a rice measurer in a rice shop in the southern city. Last year, through matchmaker Shen Guisheng, he engaged Wang Yusheng's daughter, A'san, who lives in Longhua and works as a carpenter, to be his wife. They had already chosen March 28th of this year as the wedding date. Recently, Hou was distributing wedding invitations to relatives and friends in preparation for the upcoming wedding. Unexpectedly, the bride did not want to marry Hou and asked her parents to cancel the engagement. Her parents refused. The other day, Ke San secretly ran away. Wang searched without success. With the wedding date approaching, Wang had no choice but to claim that his daughter was seriously ill and could not get married, and asked the matchmaker to inform the groom's family to postpone the wedding. Hou was suspicious and inquired of Wang's neighbors, learning that his fiancée had indeed run away. He summoned the matchmaker to his home and told him the situation, saying that the wedding date had been set and could not be changed at will, and that he was determined to marry her. Wang had no choice but to discuss returning the betrothal gifts and paying some compensation to cancel the marriage, requesting 400 yuan in compensation. Wang agreed to pay 100 yuan. The matchmaker, Shen Guisheng, mediated without success.

The Yang Chen Family Initiates Another Lawsuit Regarding Personal Matters: One Advocates Divorce, One Advocates Cohabitation

Yang Chengkun, the owner of the Mingli Inn on Wuzhen Road in Zhabei, hired Fang Guisheng as a matchmaker in the 13th year of the Republic of China to marry Chen Xirong's daughter, A'hua (also known as Yinhua), from his hometown of Shaoxing Yuyao, spending 300 yuan on betrothal gifts. Since A'hua repeatedly ran back to her mother's house, A'hua sent a letter to Yang Chengkun demanding 240 yuan for food expenses, and Chen Xirong collected 100 yuan in membership fees under Yang Chengkun's name from a certain place in his hometown of Shaoxing. Therefore, Yang Chengkun hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit in the Criminal Court of the District Court against his father-in-law, Chen Xirong, for fraud and "releasing white doves" (a term for spreading false information), his mother-in-law, Chen Wen, for possessing stolen goods, Chen A'hua for stealing clothes, and Fang Guisheng for colluding to "release white doves." After the Criminal Court's trial, Chen Xirong and others were found not guilty. Yang, dissatisfied, appealed. The other day, Chief Judge Feng and judges Chen and Zuo opened a court for final arguments and set the date for judgment on the 18th of this month. Chen A'hua also hired lawyer Yan Yinwu to file a divorce lawsuit in the Civil Court of the District Court, claiming that she could not bear the abuse and requesting permission to divorce. Yang Chengkun hired lawyer Wang Xianggu to file a defense and counterclaim requesting cohabitation. Judge Pang opened the court yesterday. Chen Yinhua testified that she was 23 years old, from Yuyao, and currently lived with her mother at the Senda Coal Shop at No. 25 Nancang Street outside Xiaonanmen, because she could not bear the hardship, so she left. As for demanding food expenses, it was because her mother's family was in a difficult situation, but Yang ignored it, so she had no choice but to request a divorce. Yang Chengkun testified that he was 26 years old and worked as a typesetter. After he married the plaintiff on November 16th of the 13th year of the Republic of China, they were harmonious at first, but on April 18th of the following year, the plaintiff ran away with her belongings. Later, he found her at her mother's house and brought her back. On July 3rd of the 15th year, she ran away twice and could not be found. Now she has sent a letter demanding food expenses, and the defendant has learned that she is still with her mother. Therefore, he filed a lawsuit in the Criminal Court of your court. He does not want a divorce and requests cohabitation. The judge obtained the testimony and attempted reconciliation, repeatedly persuading the plaintiff to return to her husband, but the plaintiff firmly refused. Then the arguments began, with the lawyers hired by both parties arguing back and forth. Prosecutor Wang also came to court to express his opinion. The judge then declared the arguments concluded and set the date for sentencing at 1:00 PM on the 19th of this month.

Wife Accuses Husband of Abuse and Assault: Ni, Wife of Chen Bingnan from Shaoxing, Files Lawsuit in Provisional Court

Ni, the 24-year-old wife of Chen Bingnan from Shaoxing, recently filed a lawsuit in the Provisional Court accusing Chen of abuse and abandonment, stating that Chen initially claimed to be a comprador in a foreign firm. Seven days after the marriage, she was forced to pawn her clothes and jewelry to make a living. If she refused, he would beat her. On March 18th of last year, Chen colluded with his brother, Chen Bingquan, to demand 1,000 yuan. When she refused to give it, they beat her. On December 23rd, Chen again ordered Bingquan to force her to divorce. She reported it to the Huishi Police Station at that time. On January 27th of this year, he again resorted to violence and humiliation when she refused to give him money, causing her to fall from the third floor to the second floor, injuring her left rib and right cheekbone. She also injured her pregnancy. She has a medical certificate from Jisheng Hospital as proof. She requested that he be prosecuted according to the law. Chen also hired lawyer Lu Qi to file a statement arguing that they had been a loving couple for two years and that she often went to entertainment venues and was flirtatious and that the accusations were untrue. He requested that her lawsuit be rejected. The court, based on the statement, issued a summons order signed by Judge Sun, ordering the arrest and reporting of both parties for a hearing in the coming days.

Worker Commits Suicide Due to Economic Pressure: Wang Xiaoshan from Jiangbei Hangs Himself

Wang Xiaoshan, a 20-year-old man from Jiangbei, whose father runs a firewood and charcoal shop at No. 137 Binlang Road in western Shanghai. Wang used to be a worker in the internal and external cotton mills, but he was dismissed last winter and has been unemployed ever since. With nothing to do, his finances became strained, and he became depressed. He suddenly had a suicidal thought and hanged himself in his room at around 11:45 PM the other night. After being discovered by his family, they sent a letter asking for help, but it was too late, and he could not be revived. They immediately reported it to the Putuo Road Police Station, which ordered officer No. 228 to send the body to Renji Hospital for an autopsy.

Man Attempts Suicide by Drowning: Rescued by Police Officers of the Water Patrol Team

At around 7:15 PM last night, patrolling police officers and sailors of Squad B of the Second Branch of the Zhabei Water Patrol Team were patrolling near the pier in front of the Laohuzao Stove east of Dafengmiao Factory in Tanzhwan when they saw a man jump into the river to commit suicide. They immediately rescued him from the water and changed his wet clothes. The man identified himself as Yu Zhonghua, from Changzhou, 23 years old. He and his brother, Zhongqing, worked as employees at the Wang Yuantai leather trunk shop at the intersection of Bintang Lane and Shanxi Road in the Public Concession. This morning (16th) at around 10:00 AM, he felt depressed and walked along the Suzhou River. He became disoriented and accidentally fell into the water. His parents are still in Changzhou. He did not reveal the specific details.

Unexpected Disaster While Watching Seizure of Opium: Wang Daxizi Falsely Accused of Stealing Opium; Xu Dajunzi Organizes Mob to Assault

Wang Daxizi, originally from Jiangbei, works as an employee at the Gongxing Salt Shop on Yuanfang Road in Hongkou. The owner of the shop, Jiang Si, learned that the Yuhe Steamer of the Yuhe Foreign Firm had arrived at the port yesterday at around 4:00 PM and ordered Wang to collect the salt bill from the ship. Shortly afterward, soldiers from the Garrison Headquarters arrived, claiming that they had received a tip that a large amount of opium was hidden in the ship's hold. After the soldiers boarded the ship, they searched it and seized a quantity of opium. Wang was watching from the side. After it was over, Wang returned to the shop for dinner. Just as he was about to go to bed, he learned that the "Little Company," a opium-dealing organization on Huaji Road, founded by the notorious gangster Xu Dajunzi and his sidekick Bei Xiaogouzi, claimed that the seized opium was Xu's property, smuggled from Hankou. Someone reported to Xu that Wang had stolen two pieces of opium when the troops searched the ship. After hearing the report, Xu led several hooligans, secretly armed with sharp blades, to Wang to demand their return. Wang denied it. Xu shouted loudly, and the hooligans pulled out their sharp blades and slashed Wang's head seven or eight times, causing him to bleed profusely and lose consciousness. Seeing that they had caused a disaster, the perpetrators fled. The shop owner ordered someone to take Wang to Tongren Hospital for treatment. His injuries are said to be critical.

Body Brother Arrests Perpetrator: Accomplice in Wang Baoshan Murder Case

Wang Baoshan, from Yancheng in Hubei, was shot and killed by his enemy Dai Ruzhao and his gang. The case is being investigated by the Shanghai District Court. Zhu Zixiang, an accomplice in the same case, was seen by the brother of the deceased, Wang Tingzhang, in front of the Wing On Company the other day. The enemy's road was narrow, and he was arrested and brought to the police station. He was brought back for questioning by the Third Division of the Fifth District and denied it. He was sent to the District Court yesterday for investigation.

Robber Lu Shizhang Imprisoned for Five Years: Lu Shizhang Organized Gang to Rob Chen A'tang's House in French Concession

Robber Lu Shizhang and his gang broke into Chen A'tang's house in the French Concession with weapons last month. The victim shouted loudly for help, and the robbers panicked and fled empty-handed. The victim reported the robbery to the police and asked them to investigate. Now, the special investigation unit of the French Police Department has apprehended the robber Lu and brought him to the police station. The other day, he was sent to the French Court for questioning. The plaintiff, Chen A'tang, complained about the robbery and presented a bullet left behind by the robbers as evidence. Lu Shizhang confessed to the robbery. The Chinese and Western officials sentenced Lu to five years in the Western Prison and permanent expulsion from the concession upon completion of the sentence.

Fire to be Investigated Further: The French Concession's Jin Shenfu Road Yuanhe Pawnshop Caught Fire

The French Concession's Jin Shenfu Road Yuanhe Pawnshop recently caught fire. The fire was extinguished by the fire brigade, as reported in previous newspapers. The other day, the police summoned the pawnshop's manager, Yu Zhaosheng, to the French Court for questioning. The pawnshop hired lawyer Ba He to defend him, stating that the pawnshop's business was doing well and had been very prosperous recently. The fire was suspected to have been caused by someone deliberately. He requested that someone be sent to investigate. The Chinese and Western officials, after reviewing the statement, approved the dispatch of someone to investigate and review the case.

Russian Woman Arrested for Drunkenly Causing Trouble: Russian Woman Yilin Maixiang Detained

Russian woman Yilin Maixiang was arrested by Russian officer No. 251 of the Huishi Police Department for drunkenly causing trouble and assaulting pedestrians in the Broadway area at around 10:00 PM yesterday. She was taken to the police station and, after being informed by the police chief, was ordered to be transferred to the women's detention center for temporary detention, pending trial by the court.

Liquor Store Robbery Awaits Sentencing: Accountant Flees After Incident; Embezzles More Than 3,000 Yuan in Public Funds

The Broadway Yucheng Liquor Store was robbed at gunpoint on January 28th. One robber was killed by the police, and another, Huang A'ying, was captured alive. The store's accountant, Wang Yichang, abandoned his post and fled after the incident, as reported in previous newspapers. The other day, the police brought the robber Huang to the Provisional Court for further trial. According to Lu Yanping, a clerk at the liquor store, Wang Yichang sent a letter to the store the day after he fled, saying that the amount he owed was recorded in the books and could be verified. Upon inspection, it was found that he owed more than 3,000 yuan. When questioned, Huang A'ying stated that the stolen money and firearms belonged to Lin Asheng, who was killed. Judge Xu, after the trial, ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody pending sentencing on a scheduled date.

Gathering for Gambling and Skimming Profits: Sentenced to One Month of Detention and a Fine of 20 Yuan

The other night, Yangshupu police officers, after learning that there was a gambling den on Zhoujiazui Road, went to investigate and arrest those involved. They apprehended 29 gamblers and gambling paraphernalia and money. Jiang Shiting, the leader who organized the gambling, claimed that his elderly mother was ill and needed money for medical treatment. He invited friends to gamble and skimmed profits to meet the emergency needs. Judge Xu ruled that his statement was false and that gathering for gambling and skimming profits was prohibited by law. He sentenced Jiang to one month of detention and a fine of 20 yuan. The remaining 28 people, including Su Xueyu, were each fined 8 yuan. The gambling paraphernalia was confiscated.

Housing Dispute in Yinyu Lane to be Resolved: Residents Oppose Rent Increases After Renovation in French Concession

The houses around Yinyu Lane in the French Concession have been in dispute due to opposition to rent increases after the landlord renovated the houses. The tenants of Yinyu Lane have formed a joint association, elected responsible committee members, and appointed three rent custodians to strongly oppose the rent increases. The landlord has also agreed to make concessions and slightly reduce the rent. An agreement has been reached, and a peaceful resolution is expected within days.

Husband Encounters Runaway Wife on the Street: Turns Her and Her Lover Over to the Police

Ding Xingbang, a 36-year-old man from Xinghua, runs a firewood shop in his hometown. His wife, Yang, 37 years old, has given birth to two sons and two daughters. Because her husband's family is very poor, she became acquainted with Yu Tongsheng, a neighbor from the same village, and committed adultery more than once. Because she was in love with the affair, she ignored her husband and children and secretly eloped with Yu to Shanghai on the 23rd of last month, taking her young son Xiaolingxi with her. After her husband found out, he searched everywhere, but there was no news. Recently, someone told him the secret, so he closed the shop and took his eldest son Dalingxizi and two daughters by boat to Shanghai on the 13th of this month, staying in a hotel and visiting various places every day. There was still no news. Yesterday at about 2:00 PM, Ding and his children happened to encounter Shi at the Shuishange area outside Xiaonanmen. Her young son Xiaolingxi and Yu were also walking together. Ding was angry when he saw them and immediately went up to grab them, calling for Wang Mao, a guard at the 14th station, to come. They were taken back to the Third Branch of the First District. The head of the Jin branch ordered them to be temporarily detained pending investigation.

Difficult to Visit Longhua Temple: Tourists Blocked by Troops

Longhua Temple in the southwest of this city is a famous ancient temple. Every spring, tourists flock to visit. Yesterday was a Sunday, and there were many tourists, but they were blocked by the troops stationed there. Whether pilgrims or tourists, they were not allowed to enter. Even dozens of foreigners with cameras and families were turned away and had to return disappointed.

Hiding Adulterous Wife: Man Arrested in Tanzi Kou, Zhabei

Wan Qijun, a native of Yancheng, Zhabei, arrested his neighbor Hu Changshan and the witness Zhang Pan and brought them to the Fourth District Headquarters, accusing them, saying that yesterday morning he and his wife Sun were talking in the room when the defendant Hu Changshan suddenly broke into his room, saying that his tenant Wang San had something to discuss with him. He believed it to be true and went, but Wang did not call him, so he returned home. Unexpectedly, Hu came again to call him after a while, so he lingered for a long time before returning. His wife suddenly disappeared, so he asked Zhang Pan, who lived with him, and learned that a little old man had deliberately asked Hu to call him out and secretly led his wife away and hid her. He asked the headquarters to investigate. Hu said that he had called the plaintiff out because his friend Wang San wanted to buy land to build a house and asked him to discuss the price, and now his wife had suddenly disappeared, and he really didn't know the situation. When questioned, the witness Zhang Pan confessed that it was true that Hu's friend, a little old man from Fujian, had called her niece to send three yuan to Wan's wife, but she didn't know what it was for. The director believed that Hu was suspected of colluding to hide Wan's wife and should be sent to the bureau for questioning.

Detectives Arrest Five Robbers: Five Robbers Arrested in Southern City

Dong Mingde, leader of the detectives in the Southern City District, and detectives Yuan Haishan, Lv Anpu, Cai Ziqing, Yu Maolong, and Ren Shouzi learned that a robber was hiding in a house at No. 9 Fuxingli, Beizhangjia Alley, Southern City. They immediately went to the address and arrested the robber and brought him to the district. During the preliminary trial by the district chief, the robber identified himself as Zhong Jinrong, 24 years old, from Wuxi, and confessed to organizing Zhang Guibao, Li Haoliang, Wang Guangqi, and Qiu Xiaocai to rob the house of Xu Yongsheng at No. 5 Tongli on the 7th of this month, carrying a fake pistol. At that time, he was a neighbor and knew him slightly, so he was guarding the door to prevent them from being seen. As a result, they robbed three fur coats and more than 200 yuan in cash. He also confessed to robbing twice in the French Concession last month with Zhang and others. The district chief immediately sent the original detectives to No. 182 Fumin Road to arrest Zhang Guibao and Li Haoliang, two robbers, and recovered a fake pistol. After bringing them to the district, they went to No. 15 Zhangjia Alley to continue to capture Wang Guangqi and brought him back. On the way, they met Qiu Xiaocai. Qiu did not see the detectives, so he greeted Wang and others. The detectives heard him and immediately went up to arrest Qiu and brought him back. During the preliminary trial by the district chief, Zhang Gui confessed that he was 21 years old and a local, Li Haoliang was 21 years old, from Shanghai, and lived in Xiqiaojumen Road outside the West Gate, Wang Guangqi was 23 years old, from Rugao, and Qiu Xiaocai was 22 years old, from Changshu, and worked as a clerk in a car dealership on Xianji Road. The others confessed the same as Zhong. Since the matter involved robbery, they were ordered to prepare a document and submit it to the Third Division of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for questioning.

Two People Fighting in the Street Over a Woman: Both Detained for Fighting

At about 1:00 PM last night, two people were fighting near Meiyuan Road in Zhabei and refused to stop. The police officer stationed there went up to inquire and learned that it was due to fighting over a woman. They arrested them and brought them to the Fourth District Headquarters. According to one of them, Niu Wanyi, a 29-year-old from Yancheng, he was watching a play at the Yangzhou Theater when a woman sat next to him and he talked to her for a while. The other man accused him of flirting. When he left the theater, the other man slapped him a few times. He was unwilling to be humiliated for no reason, so he fought back. The other man, Yang Guang'en, a 19-year-old from Taizhou, said that he was watching a play with his lover when the other man made obscene jokes. He immediately reprimanded him, but he was shameless and continued to make jokes, so he went to argue with him. They disagreed and started fighting. The director believed that both parties were wrong and ordered them to be detained separately as a warning.
